Home > ALS > StorageRing > arplot_sr_with_shutters.m

arplot_sr_with_shutters

PURPOSE

arplot_sr(Month1 String, Days1, Year1, Month2 String, Days2, Year2)

SYNOPSIS

function arplot_sr(monthStr, days, year1, month2Str, days2, year2)

DESCRIPTION 

 arplot_sr(Month1 String, Days1, Year1, Month2 String, Days2, Year2)

 Plots a whole bunch of storage ring related archived data.
 Only plots data when feed forward is on.

 Example #1:  arplot_sr('January',22:24,1998);
              plots data from 1/22, 1/23, and 1/24 in 1998

 Example #2:  arplot_sr('January',28:31,1998,'February',1:4,1998);
              plots data from the last 4 days in Jan. and the first 4 days in Feb.

 See also arplot arplot_sr_report arplot_sbm

 Written by Greg Portmann & Tom Scarvie

CROSS-REFERENCE INFORMATION

This function calls:
  • arglobal Just used to make archived variables global
  • arread ARREAD - Loads one day of archived data into matlab global memory
  • arselect ARSELECT - Return the archived data for a group on channel names
  • gap2tune GAP2TUNE - Computes the vertical tune shift for a insertion device gap change.
  • getbpmlist GETBPMLIST - Return a BPM list based on key words and sector numbers
This function is called by:

SUBFUNCTIONS

  • function ChangeAxesLabel(t, Days, DayFlag)

2254 i = find(dcct < .5);
2255 BPMx(:,i) = NaN;

2257 dcct(i) = NaN;
2258 dlogdcct = diff(log(dcct));

2260 i = find(lifetime1 < 0);
2261 lifetime1(i) = NaN;

2263 i = find(i_cam < .5);
2264 i_cam(i) = NaN;
2265 
2266 % dlogcam = mean([diff(log(i_cam(1:(end-9))));diff(log(i_cam(2:(end-8)))); ...
2267 %        diff(log(i_cam(3:(end-7))));diff(log(i_cam(4:(end-6)))); ...
2268 %        diff(log(i_cam(5:(end-5))));diff(log(i_cam(6:(end-4)))); ...
2269 %        diff(log(i_cam(7:(end-3))));diff(log(i_cam(8:(end-2)))); ...

2271 
2272 logcam = log(i_cam);lifetime2=[];
2273 
2274 tic;
2275 for loop = 1:(length(logcam)-15)
2276     fitpar = polyfit(t(loop:(loop+15))/60/60,logcam(loop:(loop+15)),1);
2277     stdfit = std(logcam(loop:(loop+15))-polyval(fitpar,t(loop:(loop+15))/60/60));
2278     remindex = find(abs(logcam(loop:(loop+15))-polyval(fitpar,t(loop:(loop+15))/60/60))>2.5*stdfit);
2279     logcam(loop+remindex-1)=NaN;
2280     fitpar = polyfit(t(loop:(loop+15))/60/60,logcam(loop:(loop+15)),1);
2281     lifetime2(loop) = -1/fitpar(1);
2282 end
2283 cam_fit_time = toc;
2284 %fprintf('  %.1f seconds to fit cam bucket lifetime\n', cam_fit_time);

3479 % Subtract the golden orbit from Bergoz BPMs

3482     BPMy(:,i) = BPMy(:,i) - BPMyGolden;

3490     i = find(sum(GapEnable) < 3);   % Why 3, just because sometimes 1 or 2 gaps are enabled for testing.
3491 else

5822 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
5823 function ChangeAxesLabel(t, Days, DayFlag)
5824 xaxis([0 max(t)]);
5825 
5826 if DayFlag
5827     if size(Days,2) > 1
5828         Days = Days'; % Make a column vector
5829     end
5830 
5831     MaxDay = round(max(t));
5832     set(gca,'XTick',[0:MaxDay]');
5833     %xaxis([0 MaxDay]);
5834 
5835     if length(Days) < MaxDay-1
5836         % Days were skipped
5837         set(gca,'XTickLabel',strvcat(num2str([0:MaxDay-1]'+Days(1)),' '));
5838     else
5839         % All days plotted
5840         set(gca,'XTickLabel',strvcat(num2str(Days),' '));
5841     end
5842 
5843     XTickLabelString = get(gca,'XTickLabel');
5844     if MaxDay < 20
5845         % ok
5846     elseif MaxDay < 40
5847         set(gca,'XTick',[0:2:MaxDay]');
5848         set(gca,'XTickLabel',XTickLabelString(1:2:MaxDay-1,:));
5849     elseif MaxDay < 63
5850         set(gca,'XTick',[0:3:MaxDay]');
5851         set(gca,'XTickLabel',XTickLabelString(1:3:MaxDay-1,:));
5852     elseif MaxDay < 80
5853         set(gca,'XTick',[0:4:MaxDay]');
5854         set(gca,'XTickLabel',XTickLabelString(1:4:MaxDay-1,:));
5855     end
5856 end
